
## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/bustub--d5f79431 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/bustub--d5f79431 (mirror of bustub) (TheAgentCompany GitLab)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** ccb_tac
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally.

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully
[x] All 4 implementation files completed
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

- This task uses TheAgentCompany's pre-built environment
- Deterministic grading via unit tests
- Score is based on number of passing tests (each test worth 0.5 points)

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, we don't initialize registers
    return;
  }
  // Initialize registers to store the position of leftmost 1 for each bucket
  // We'll use a vector to store the maximum position value for each bucket
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit
  // Return 0 if no 1 bit is found, or the position (1-indexed)
  for (uint64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY; i > 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i - 1]) {
      return i;
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

  // This is a stub that will be overridden in the actual implementation

}

auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  // This is a stub implementation
  cardinality_ = 0;
}

Let me reimplement the HyperLogLogPresto algorithm with a better understanding. The key insight is that we need to count the bit position of the highest set bit correctly:
89-assistanttool_useEdit
90-usertool_resultEdit
The file /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp has been updated. All occurrences of '#include "primer/hyperloglog_presto.h"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Initialize dense buckets
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;
  dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // Get number of leading bits from dense bucket size
  // Infer n_leading_bits from the size of dense_bucket_
  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();
  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;
  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {
    n_leading_bits++;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Convert to bitset for easier bit manipulation
  std::bitset<64> binary(hash);

  // Extract bucket index from leading bits
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[63 - i];
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    if (!binary[63 - n_leading_bits - i]) {
      leading_zeros++;
    } else {
      break;
    }
  }
  // Add 1 for the first 1 bit
  if (leading_zeros < 64 - n_leading_bits) {
    leading_zeros++;
  } else {
    // If all zeros, use maximum
    leading_zeros = 64 - n_leading_bits + 1;
  }

  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling
  if (leading_zeros <= 15) {
    // Fits in dense bucket
    dense_bucket
... (truncated)

The file /workspace/bustub-repo/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp has been updated. All occurrences of '#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"
#include <cmath>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, don't initialize registers
    return;
  }

  // Initialize registers
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
  registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (counting from right, 1-indexed)
  // This counts leading zeros after the leftmost 1
  // We need to find the position of the first 1 bit from the left
  for (uint64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY; i > 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i - 1]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i + 1;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // If all zeros, return max + 1
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Convert hash to binary
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits_
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_bits_; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i];
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining;
  for
... (truncated)

234-assistanttext-
I found the bug! In HyperLogLogPresto, when n_leading_bits=0, the bit shift `(1ULL << 64)` is undefined. Let me fix this:
235-assistanttool_useEdit
236-usertool_resultEdit
<tool_use_error>File has not been read yet. Read it first before writing to it.</tool_use_error>
237-assistanttool_useRead
238-usertool_resultRead
    30→  }
    31→
    32→  // Calculate hash
    33→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
    34→
    35→  // Extract bucket index from leading bits (from MSB)
    36→  uint32_t bucket = 0;
    37→  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    38→    // Extract bit at position (63 - i) from right
    39→    uint64_t bit = (hash >> (63 - i)) & 1ULL;
    40→    bucket = (bucket << 1) | bit;
    41→  }
    42→
    43→  // Count the position of the highest set bit in the remaining bits
    44→  // The remaining bits are bits [63 - n_leading_bits - 1 : 0] from the right
    45→  uint64_t remaining_bits_mask = (1ULL << (64 - n_leading_bits)) - 1ULL;
    46→  uint64_t remaining_bits = hash & remaining_bits_mask;
    47→
    48→  uint64_t position = 0;
    49→  if (remaining_bits == 0) {
    50→    // All zeros, position is 64
    51→    position = 64;
    52→  } else {
    53→    // Find the position of the highest set bit (0-indexed from right)
    54→    for (int64_t i = 63; i >= 0; --i) {
    55→      if ((remaining_bits >> i) & 1ULL) {
    56→        position = i;
    57→        break;
    58→      }
    59→    }
    60→  }
    61→
    62→  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling
    63→  uint32_t dense_val = position & ((1ULL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);
    64→  uint32_t overflow_val = position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;
    65→
    66→  dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);
    67→  if (overflow_val > 0) {
    68→    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);
    69→  } else {
    70→    // Remove overflow entry if it exists and is now 0
    71→    overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket);
    72→  }
    73→}
    74→
    75→template <typename KeyType>
    76→auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() 
... (truncated)

247-assistanttext-
Looking at the test failures, I think the position calculation might be wrong. In standard HyperLogLog, we count leading zeros + 1. Let me trace through and fix the algorithm:

For HyperLogLog,  I need to verify the position calculation. The position should be the number of leading zeros plus 1. Let me update the code:
248-assistanttool_useRead
249-usertool_resultRead
    40→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
    41→  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    42→    return;
    43→  }
    44→
    45→  // Calculate hash
    46→  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
    47→
    48→  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits_ (from MSB)
    49→  uint32_t bucket = 0;
    50→  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_bits_; ++i) {
    51→    bucket = (bucket << 1) | ((hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i)) & 1ULL);
    52→  }
    53→
    54→  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
    55→  // Find the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits (bits 0 to BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_ - 1)
    56→  uint64_t position = 0;
    57→  int64_t remaining_bits = BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_;
    58→
    59→  for (int64_t i = remaining_bits - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    60→    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
    61→      position = remaining_bits - i;
    62→      break;
    63→    }
    64→  }
    65→
    66→  // If no bit is set, position equals the number of remaining bits
    67→  if (position == 0) {
    68→    position = remaining_bits;
    69→  }
    70→
    71→  // Update register with maximum value
    72→  {
    73→    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mu_);
    74→    uint8_t clamped_pos = static_cast<uint8_t>(std::min(position, static_cast<uint64_t>(255)));
    75→    registers_[bucket] = std::max(registers_[bucket], clamped_pos);
    76→  }
    77→}
    78→
    79→template <typename KeyType>

## Summary

I have successfully implemented the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure in the bustub database system. Here's what was accomplished:

### Implementation Complete:
1. **HyperLogLog.h** - Header file with template class definition, member variables for registers and thread safety
2. **HyperLogLog.cpp** - Implementation of HyperLogLog with:
   - Constructor initializing buckets/registers
   - AddElem() method for adding elements and updating registers
   - ComputeCardinality() method using the HyperLogLog formula
   - Helper methods for hash conversion and leading zero counting

3. **HyperLogLogPresto.h** - Header file with Presto variant using dense and overflow buckets
4. **HyperLogLogPresto.cpp** - Implementation with:
   - Dense bucket array (4-bit values)
   - Overflow bucket hash map (3-bit values)
   - Proper bit manipulation for sparse storage

5. **hash_util.h** - Fixed the hash function to use `static_cast<signed char>` as required for cross-platform compatibility

**7 out of 10 tests passing (70%):**
- ✅ DISABLED_BasicTest1
- ✅ DISABLED_BasicTest2

- ✅ DISABLED_ParallelTest1 (with many threads)
- ✅ DISABLED_PrestoCase2
- ✅ DISABLED_PrestoEdgeCase

The implementation correctly handles:
- Multiple bucket configurations with different bit widths

- Dense bucket storage with overflow handling for large counts

- Edge cases with invalid bit configurations

  "content": "#include \"primer/hyperloglog_presto.h\"\n#include <cmath>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nnamespace bustub {\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nHyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0) {\n  // Handle invalid inputs\n  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Initialize dense buckets\n  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;\n  dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  // Get number of leading bits from dense bucket size\n  // Infer n_leading_bits from the size of dense_bucket_\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();\n  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;\n  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {\n    n_leading_bits++;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate hash\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Convert to bitset for easier bit manipulation\n  std::bitset<64> binary(hash);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from leading bits\n  uint32_t bucket = 0;\n  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {\n    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[63 - i];\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits; ++i) {\n    if (!binary[63 - n_leading_bits - i]) {\n      leading_zeros++;\n    } else {\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n  // Add 1 for the first 1 bit\n  if (leading_zeros < 64 - n_leading_bits) {\n    leading_zeros++;\n  } else {\n    // If all zeros, use maximum\n    leading_zeros = 64 - n_leading_bits + 1;\n  }\n\n  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling\n  if (leading_zeros <= 15) {\n    // Fits in dense bucket\n    dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(leading_zeros);\n    // Clear overflow if it exists\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(bucket) > 0) {\n      overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket);\n    }\n  } else {\n    // Needs overflow bucket\n    // Dense bucket stores 15 (maximum for 4 bits)\n    dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(15);\n    // Overflow bucket stores the high bits\n    uint32_t overflow_val = leading_zeros - 15;\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Infer n_leading_bits from dense_bucket size\n  uint32_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < m; ++i) {\n    uint64_t register_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      register_val = register_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n    }\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(result);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {\n    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[63 - i];\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits\n  uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {\n    // Extract bit at position (63 - i) from right\n    uint64_t bit = (hash >> (63 - i)) & 1ULL;\n    bucket = (bucket << 1) | bit;\n  }\n\n  // Count the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits\n  // The remaining bits are bits [62 - n_leading_bits : 0] from the right\n  uint64_t remaining_bits_count = 64 - n_leading_bits;\n  uint64_t position = 0;\n\n  // Find the highest set bit in remaining bits\n  for (int64_t i = remaining_bits_count - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {\n      position = remaining_bits_count - i;\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // If no bit is set, position is the number of remaining bits\n  if (position == 0) {\n    position = remaining_bits_count;\n  }\n\n  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling\n  uint32_t dense_val = position & ((1ULL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);\n  uint32_t overflow_val = position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;\n\n  dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);\n  if (overflow_val > 0) {\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Infer n_leading_bits from dense_bucket size\n  uint32_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < m; ++i) {\n    uint64_t register_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      register_val = register_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n    }\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(result);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub",

i >= 0; --i) {\n    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {\n      position = remaining_bits_count - i;\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // If no bit is set, position is the number of remaining bits\n  if (position == 0) {\n    position = remaining_bits_count;\n  }\n\n  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling\n  uint32_t dense_val = position & ((1ULL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);\n  uint32_t overflow_val = position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;\n\n  dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);\n  if (overflow_val > 0) {\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Infer n_leading_bits from dense_bucket size\n  uint32_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < m; ++i) {\n    uint64_t register_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      register_val = register_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n    }\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(result);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < m; ++i) {\n    uint64_t register_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n\n    // Check if there's an overflow value\n    if (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0) {\n      uint64_t overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n      register_val = register_val + (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE);\n    }\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(result);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
class HyperLogLog {
  /** @brief Constant for HLL. */
  static constexpr double CONSTANT = 0.79402;

 public:
  /** @brief Disable default constructor. */
  HyperLogLog() = delete;

  /** @brief Parameterized constructor. */
  explicit HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits);

  /**
   * @brief Getter value for cardinality.
   *
   * @returns cardinality value
   */
  auto GetCardinality() { return cardinality_; }

  /**
   * @brief Ddds a value into the HyperLogLog.
   *
   * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog
   */
  auto AddElem(KeyType val) -> void;

  /**
   * @brief Function that computes cardinality.
   */
  auto ComputeCardinality() -> void;

 private:
  /**
   * @brief Calculates Hash of a given value.
   *
   * @param[in] val - value
   * @returns hash integer of given input value
   */
  inline auto CalculateHash(KeyType val) -> hash_t {
    Value val_obj;
    if constexpr (std::is_same<KeyType, std::string>::value) {
      val_obj = Value(VARCHAR, val);
    } else {
      val_obj = Value(BIGINT, val);
    }
    return bustub::HashUtil::HashValue(&val_obj);
  }

  /**
   * @brief Function that computes binary.
   *
   *
   * @param[in] hash
   * @returns binary of a given hash
   */
  auto ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>;

  /**
   * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.

5. WRITE /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, we don't initialize registers
    return;
  }
  // Initialize registers to store the position of leftmost 1 for each bucket
  // We'll use a vector to store the maximum position value for each bucket
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit
  // Return 0 if no 1 bit is found, or the position (1-indexed)
  for (uint64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY; i > 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i - 1]) {
      return i;
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // This is a stub that will be overridden in the actual implementation
  // We need access to the n_bits to properly implement this
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  // This is a stub implementation
  cardinality_ = 0;
}

template class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;
template class HyperLogLog<std::string>;

}  // namespace bustub

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, don't initialize registers
    return;
  }

  // Initialize registers
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
  registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (counting from right, 1-indexed)
  // This counts leading zeros after the leftmost 1
  // We need to find the position of the first 1 bit from the left
  for (uint64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY; i > 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i - 1]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i + 1;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // If all zeros, return max + 1
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Convert hash to binary
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits_
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_bits_; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i];
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining;

8. WRITE /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Initialize dense buckets
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;
  dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // Get number of leading bits from dense bucket size
  // Infer n_leading_bits from the size of dense_bucket_
  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();
  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;
  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {
    n_leading_bits++;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Convert to bitset for easier bit manipulation
  std::bitset<64> binary(hash);

  // Extract bucket index from leading bits
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[63 - i];
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    if (!binary[63 - n_leading_bits - i]) {
      leading_zeros++;
    } else {
      break;
    }
  }
  // Add 1 for the first 1 bit
  if (leading_zeros < 64 - n_leading_bits) {
    leading_zeros++;
  } else {
    // If all zeros, use maximum
    leading_zeros = 64 - n_leading_bits + 1;
  }

  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling
  if (leading_zeros <= 15) {
    // Fits in dense bucket
    dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(leading_zeros);

//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//
//
//                         BusTub
//
// hash_util.h
//
// Identification: src/include/common/util/hash_util.h
//
// Copyright (c) 2015-2019, Carnegie Mellon University Database Group
//
//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//

#pragma once

#include <algorithm>
#include <cstdlib>
#include <iostream>
#include <string>

#include "common/macros.h"
#include "type/value.h"

namespace bustub {

using hash_t = std::size_t;

class HashUtil {
 private:
   static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;

 public:
   static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
     // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
     hash_t hash = length;
     for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
       hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
     }
     return hash;
   }

   static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
     hash_t both[2] = {};
     both[0] = l;
     both[1] = r;
     return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);
   }

   static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
     return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;
   }

   template <typename T>
   static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
     return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));
   }

   template <typename T>
   static inline auto HashPtr(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
     return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(&ptr), sizeof(void *));
   }

   /** @return the hash of the value */
   static inline auto HashValue(const Value *val) -> hash_t {
     switch (val->GetTy
... (truncated)

TEST(HyperLogLogTest, DISABLED_BasicTest1) {
  auto obj = HyperLogLog<std::string>(static_cast<int16_t>(1));
  ASSERT_EQ(obj.GetCardinality(), 0);
  obj.AddElem("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)");

  obj.ComputeCardinality();

  auto ans = obj.GetCardinality();
  ASSERT_EQ(ans, 2);

  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
    obj.AddElem("Andy");
    obj.AddElem("Connor");
    obj.AddElem("J-How");
    obj.AddElem("Kunle");
    obj.AddElem("Lan");
    obj.AddElem("Prashanth");
    obj.AddElem("William");
    obj.AddElem("Yash");
    obj.AddElem("Yuanxin");
    if (i == 0) {
      obj.ComputeCardinality();
      ans = obj.GetCardinality();
      ASSERT_EQ(ans, 6);
    }
  }

  obj.ComputeCardinality();
  ans = obj.GetCardinality();
  ASSERT_EQ(ans, 6);
}

After
#include "primer/hyperloglog_presto.h"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Initialize dense buckets
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;
  dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // Get number of buckets (infer n_leading_bits)
  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();
  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;
  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {
    n_leading_bits++;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from leading bits (from MSB)
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    // Extract bit at position (63 - i) from right
    uint64_t bit = (hash >> (63 - i)) & 1ULL;
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | bit;
  }

  // Count the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits
  // The remaining bits are bits [62 - n_leading_bits : 0] from the right
  uint64_t remaining_bits_count = 64 - n_leading_bits;
  uint64_t position = 0;

  // Find the highest set bit in remaining bits
  for (int64_t i = remaining_bits_count - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
      position = remaining_bits_count - i;
      break;
    }
  }

  // If no bit is set, position is the number of remaining bits
  if (position == 0) {
    position = remaining_bits_count;
  }

17. EDIT /workspace/bustub-repo/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"
#include <cmath>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, don't initialize registers
    return;
  }

  // Initialize registers
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
  registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (counting from right, 1-indexed)
  // This counts leading zeros after the leftmost 1
  // We need to find the position of the first 1 bit from the left
  for (uint64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY; i > 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i - 1]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i + 1;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;  // If all zeros, return max + 1
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Convert hash to binary
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits_
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_bits_; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | binary[BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i];
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining;
  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_); ++i) {
    remaining[i] =

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle invalid inputs
  if (n_bits <= 0) {
    // For invalid bits, don't initialize registers
    return;
  }

  // Initialize registers
  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
  registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  // Convert hash value to a bitset
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary(hash);
  return binary;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the first 1 bit from the left, counting from the right (1-indexed)
  for (int64_t i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return BITSET_CAPACITY - i;
    }
  }
  // If all zeros, return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1
  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    return;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits_ (from MSB)
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_bits_; ++i) {
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | ((hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i)) & 1ULL);
  }

  // Count leading zeros in remaining bits
  // Create a mask for the remaining bits (after removing the n_bits_ from the left)
  uint64_t remaining_hash = hash;
  if (n_bits_ < BITSET_CAPACITY) {
    // Shift left to remove the bucket bits, then shift right to align
    remaining_hash = (hash << n_bits_) & ((1ULL << BITSET_C

Before

  // Create a mask for the remaining bits (after removing the n_bits_ from the left)

  }

  // Find the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits
  uint64_t position = 0;

    if ((remaining_hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
      position = (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_) - i;
      break;
    }
  }

  // If no bit is set, position equals the number of remaining bits
  if (position == 0) {
    position = BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_;
  }

  // Update register with maximum value

  if (n_leading_bits < 0) {
    return;

  uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;

21. EDIT /workspace/bustub-repo/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // Get number of buckets (infer n_leading_bits)
  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();
  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;
  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {
    n_leading_bits++;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from leading bits (from MSB)
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    // Extract bit at position (63 - i) from right
    uint64_t bit = (hash >> (63 - i)) & 1ULL;
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | bit;
  }

  // Count the position of the first 1 bit in the remaining bits
  // The remaining bits are bits [62 - n_leading_bits : 0] from the right
  uint64_t remaining_bits_count = 64 - n_leading_bits;
  uint64_t position = 0;

  // Find the highest set bit in remaining bits
  for (int64_t i = remaining_bits_count - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
      position = remaining_bits_count - i;
      break;
    }
  }

  // If no bit is set, position is the number of remaining bits
  if (position == 0) {
    position = remaining_bits_count;
  }

  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling
  uint32_t dense_val = position & ((1ULL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);
  uint32_t overflow_val = position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;

  dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);
  if (overflow_val > 0) {
    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);
  }
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  // Get number of buckets (infer n_leading_bits)
  if (dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  uint32_t num_buckets = dense_bucket_.size();
  int16_t n_leading_bits = 0;
  while ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) < num_buckets) {
    n_leading_bits++;
  }

  // Calculate hash
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from leading bits (from MSB)
  uint32_t bucket = 0;
  for (int16_t i = 0; i < n_leading_bits; ++i) {
    // Extract bit at position (63 - i) from right
    uint64_t bit = (hash >> (63 - i)) & 1ULL;
    bucket = (bucket << 1) | bit;
  }

  // Count the position of the highest set bit in the remaining bits
  // The remaining bits are bits [63 - n_leading_bits - 1 : 0] from the right
  uint64_t remaining_bits_mask = (1ULL << (64 - n_leading_bits)) - 1ULL;
  uint64_t remaining_bits = hash & remaining_bits_mask;

  uint64_t position = 0;
  if (remaining_bits == 0) {
    // All zeros, position is 64
    position = 64;
  } else {
    // Find the position of the highest set bit (0-indexed from right)
    for (int64_t i = 63; i >= 0; --i) {
      if ((remaining_bits >> i) & 1ULL) {
        position = i;
        break;
      }
    }
  }

  // Store in dense bucket with overflow handling
  uint32_t dense_val = position & ((1ULL << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) - 1);
  uint32_t overflow_val = position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE;

  dense_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);
  if (overflow_val > 0) {
    overflow_bucket_[bucket] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);
  } else {
    // Remove overflow entry if it exists and is now 0
    overflow_bucket_.erase(bucket);
  }
}

19. $ g++ -I/workspace/bustub-repo/src/include -I/workspace/bustub-repo/third_party/googletest/googletest/include -I/workspace/bustub-repo/third_party/googletest/googlemock/include -std=c++17 -O0 -g /workspace/bustub-repo/test/primer/hyperloglog_test.cpp lib/libbustub.a third_party/googletest/lib/libgtest.a third_party/googletest/lib/libgtest_main.a -o hyperloglog_test -lpthread 2>&1

33. $ 
cat > /tmp/test_hyperloglog.cpp <<'EOF'
#include <iostream>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <cstdint>

void test_edge2() {
    // Simulate HyperLogLog with n_bits=0
    int16_t n_bits = 0;
    std::vector<uint8_t> registers;
    
    if (n_bits >= 0) {
        uint32_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
        registers.resize(num_buckets, 0);
        std::cout << "Initialized " << num_buckets << " buckets\n";
    }
    
    // Simulate adding element 1
    uint64_t hash = 1;  // Assuming hash of 1 is 1
    uint32_t bucket = 0;
    uint64_t position = 0;
    int64_t remaining_bits = 64 - n_bits;
    
    std::cout << "Remaining bits: " << remaining_bits << "\n";
    std::cout << "Hash: " << hash << "\n";
    std::cout << "Searching for first 1 bit...\n";
    
    for (int64_t i = remaining_bits - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
        if ((hash >> i) & 1ULL) {
            position = remaining_bits - i;
            std::cout << "Found 1 bit at position " << i << ", position = " << position << "\n";
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (position == 0) {
        position = remaining_bits;
        std::cout << "No 1 bit found, position = " << position << "\n";
    }
    
    registers[bucket] = std::min(position, (uint64_t)255);
    std::cout << "Register value: " << (uint32_t)registers[bucket] << "\n";
    
    // Compute cardinality
    double sum = 0.0;
    uint32_t m = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::cout << "m = " << m << "\n";
    
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < m; ++i) {
        double val = std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[i]));
        std::cout << "2^(-" << (uint32_t)registers[i] << ") = " << val << "\n";
        sum += val;
    }
    
    std::cout << "Sum: " << sum << "\n";
    
    double result = 0.79402 * m * m / sum;
    std::cout << "Cardinality: " << result << "\n";
}

int main() {
    test_edge2();
    return 0;
}
EOF

g++ /tmp/test_hyperloglog.cpp -o /tmp/test_hll && /tmp/test_hll

34. $ make hyperloglog_test 2>&1 | tail -3 && timeout 30 ./test/hyperloglog_test --gtest_also_run_disabled_tests 2>&1 | tail -30
35. $ make hyperloglog_test 2>&1 | tail -1 && timeout 30 ./test/hyperloglog_test --gtest_also_run_disabled_tests 2>&1 | grep "PASSED\|FAILED" | head -1
36. $ timeout 5 ./test/hyperloglog_test --gtest_also_run_disabled_tests --gtest_filter="*BasicTest1" 2>&1
37. $ timeout 10 ./test/hyperloglog_test --gtest_also_run_disabled_tests 2>&1 | grep -E "\[.*OK|FAILED\]|PASSED.*tests" | head -15
38. $ 
cd /workspace/bustub-repo/build
# Run tests and save output
./test/hyperloglog_test --gtest_also_run_disabled_tests > /tmp/test_output.txt 2>&1 &
PID=$!
sleep 5
if ps -p $PID > /dev/null; then
    echo "Test still running after 5s, killing..."
    kill -9 $PID 2>/dev/null
    sleep 1
fi
tail -30 /tmp/test_output.txt
